8px;\n\t\tborder-bottom: 1px solid #e5e5e5;\n\t}\n\n\t.api-page {\n\t\tposition: relative;\n\t}\n\n\t.cont.account-settings .filter a {\n\t width: 25% !important;\n}\n\n.cont .box .top-header h3 {\n\tdisplay: block !important;\n}\n\n</style>\n<!-- Table -->\n<div class=\"cont api-page account-settings\" style=\"min-height: 1994px;\">\n\n\t<div class=\"main\">\n\n\t\t<div class=\"box\">\n\n\t\t\t<div class=\"top-header\">\n\t\t\t\t<h3 style=\"display: none;\">API Documentation</h3>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t<div class=\"filter\" style=\"margin: 0px auto;\">\n\t\t\t\t<a href=\"/api\" class=\"section-toggle\">\n\t\t\t\t\tYour Apps\n\t\t\t\t</a><a class=\"active section-toggle\" href=\"/api/docs\">\n\t\t\t\t\tDocumentation\n\t\t\t\t</a><a class=\"section-toggle\" href=\"/api/explorer\">\n\t\t\t\t\tExplorer\n\t\t\t\t</a><a class=\"section-toggle\" href=\"/api/register?register=new\">\n\t\t\t\t\tAdd App\n\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t<div class=\"content api-docs-content beer-list\">\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"filters\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\tSelect an API Method\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<select id=\"sort_picker\" onchange=\"fireSwitch(this);\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#start\">Introduction</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#authentication\">Authentication</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#activityfeed\">Activity Feed</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#useractivityfeed\">User Activity Feed</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#venueactivityfeed\">Venue Activity Feed</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#beeractivityfeed\">Beer Activity Feed</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#breweryactivityfeed\">Brewery Activity Feed</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#notifications\">Notifications</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#userinfo\">User Info</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#userwishlist\">User Wish List</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#userfriends\">User Friends</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#userbadges\">User Badges</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#userbeers\">User Beers</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#breweryinfo\">Brewery Info</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#beerinfo\">Beer Info</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#venueinfo\">Venue Info</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#beersearch\">Beer Search</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#brewerysearch\">Brewery Search</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#checkin\">Checkin</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#toast\">Toast / Un-toast</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#pendingfriends\">Pending Friends</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#addfriend\">Add Friend</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#removefriend\">Remove Friend</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#acceptfriend\">Accept Friend</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#rejectfriend\">Reject Friend</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#addcomment\">Add Comment</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#removecomment\">Remove Comment</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#addwish\">Add to Wish List</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#removewish\">Remove from Wish List</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<option value=\"/api/docs#foursquarelookup\">Foursquare Lookup</option>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</select>\n\t\t\t\t\t</p>\n\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"page start\" style=\"display: block;\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>The end point for all Untappd API is <strong>https://api.untappd.com/v4</strong>. Please note that all requests, must be made over <strong>HTTPS</strong>, HTTP is not supported.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<h4>Beer List Data</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Please note that Venue Beer List (or tap list information) are <strong>NOT SUPPORTED</strong> in the Public API. If you are member of the Untappd for Business platform, please head over to <a href=\"https://docs.business.untappd.com\">https://docs.business.untappd.com</a> for documentation and how to get your API keys.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<h4>User-Agent</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Please note that you must provide a non-standard User Agent for all requests using the API (including authentication). Your user-agent can include your app name and Client ID, such as \"Greg's App (CLIENT_ID)\", however can be customized for your needs. <strong>Do not use standard user-agents, always identify your self.</strong></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<h4>Client ID / Client Secret</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>In V4 of the API, we have added Client ID and Client Secrets. You can find them on your Dashboard <a href=\"/api/dashboard\">page</a>. You Client ID is your old API Key, while the Client Secret has been added. Whenever you are making a call to the API, you MUST pass both your Client ID and Client Secret as GET params like below:</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<pre><code>https://api.untappd.com/v4/method_name?client_id=CLIENTID&amp;client_secret=CLIENTSECRET</code></pre>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>When making Authenticated requests, you will append the access token to the URL below:</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<pre><code>https://api.untappd.com/v4/method_name?access_token=ACESSTOKENHERE</code></pre>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>See the <a href=\"/api/docs#authentication\">Authentication</a> section for more details.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<h4>Responses</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>All responses in the API return JSON. The responses are very similar to other API providers, as detailed below:</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<pre><code id=\"responseJSON\">{\n  \"meta\": {\n    \"code\": 200,\n    \"response_time\": {\n      \"time\": 0,\n      \"measure\": \"seconds\"\n    }\n  },\n  \"notifications\": {},\n  \"response\": {}\n}</code></pre>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<h4>Errors</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>In the event of an error, Untappd API will return the relevant HTTP Code (500, 404, 401, etc) and have a format that looks like this:</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<pre><code id=\"errorJSON\">{\n  \"meta\": {\n    \"code\": 500,\n    \"error_detail\": \"The user has not authorized this application or the token is invalid.\",\n    \"error_type\": \"invalid_auth\",\n    \"developer_friendly\": \"The user has not authorized this application or the token is invalid.\",\n    \"response_time\": {\n      \"time\": 0,\n      \"measure\": \"seconds\"\n    }\n  }\n}</code></pre>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Please note the <code>developer_friendly</code>, may or not be in the response during an error. The best practice is to check if that attribute exists, and use that to display to your users, instead of using <code>error_detail</code>.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<h4>Rate-Limiting</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>All API applications are rate-limited to protect aganist abuse and keep the platform healthly. The default limit for API access is <strong>100 calls per hour</strong> per key. If you are using Authentication, the rate limit is applied to the user, instead of the API key.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>To check your rate-limit, we pass 2 special headers on the response that can let you know your limit:</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<pre><code>X-Ratelimit-Limit: XXXX</code><br><code>X-Ratelimit-Remaining: XXX</code></pre>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t<h3 style=\"display: none;\">Authentication</h3>\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"page authentication\" style=\"display: none;\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Authentication is handled via OAuth 2.0 Authentication. You must edit your app and add in a redirect URL that Untappd will callback after the authorization has taken place. You will receive an access token to make an authenticated calls. At this time, tokens do not expire.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<h4>Server Side Authentication (Recommended)</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>To authenticate a user, direct them to the following URL:</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<pre><code>https://untappd.com/oauth/authenticate/?client_id=CLIENTID&amp;response_type=code&amp;redirect_url=REDIRECT_URL</code></pre>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p></p>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"special-notice\"><strong>Notice:</strong> We optional support the <code>state</code> parameter that can be used in the request like below to prevent <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cross-site_request_forgery\">Cross-site Request Forgery</a>. Simple pass the <code>state</code> paramater in the authentication URL like <code>&amp;state=STATEVALUE</code> to enable this. The <code>state</code> paramater will be returned in the URL below as well once authentication occurs for you to validate.</p>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>After the user has authenticated and authorized the application, we will redirect back to the following URL:</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p></p><pre><code>http://REDIRECT_URL?code=CODE</code></pre><p></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"special-notice\"><strong>Note:</strong> Your Redirect URL (also known as the Callback URL) is set up in your App Settings. You can change it anytime by going to <a href=\"/api\">your dashboard</a> and clicking the Edit link next to link. <strong>This a required paramater for all apps that use authentication.</strong></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Taking the <code>code</code> paramater and then pass it back to the following address via GET (pass parameters via the Query String). Ensure that the REDIRECT_URL you supply in this call, is the same that was supplied in the authenticate call:</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p></p><pre><code>https://untappd.com/oauth/authorize/?client_id=CLIENTID&amp;client_secret=CLIENTSECRET&amp;response_type=code&amp;redirect_url=REDIRECT_URL&amp;code=CODE</code></pre><p></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Finally, we will send back the <code>access_token</code> that will you use for future requests, as shown in the response below:</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p></p><pre><code id=\"accessTokenJSON\">{\n  \"meta\": {\n    \"http_code\": 200\n  },\n  \"response\": {\n    \"access_token\": \"TOKEHERE\"\n  }\n}</code></pre><p></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\n\t\t\t\t<h3 class=\"method\" style=\"display: none;\">Activity Feed</h3>\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"page activityfeed\" style=\"display: none;\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<ul class=\"api-points\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><strong>Authentication</strong>: Required</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><strong>HTTP Method</strong>: <code>GET</code></li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><strong>Endpoint</strong>: <code>/v4/checkin/recent</code></li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</ul>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"api-method-description\">This method allows you the obtain all the friend check-in feed of the authenticated user. This includes only beer checkin-ins from Friends. By default it will return at max 25 records.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<h4>Parameters</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<ul class=\"api-points\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>access_token</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(string, required)</span> - The access token of the authenicated user</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>max_id</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(int, optional)</span> - The checkin ID that you want the results to start with</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>min_id</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(int, optional)</span> - Returns only checkins that are newer than this value</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>limit</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(int, optional)</span> - The number of results to return, max of 50, default is 25</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</ul>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<h4>Example Response</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p></p><pre><code class=\"activityFeedJSON\">{\n  \"checkins\": {\n    \"count\": 25,\n Feed</h3>\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"page useractivityfeed\" style=\"display: none;\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<ul class=\"api-points\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><strong>Authentication</strong>: Not Required</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><strong>HTTP Method</strong>: <code>GET</code></li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><strong>Endpoint</strong>: <code>/v4/user/checkins/USERNAME</code></li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</ul>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"special-notice\"><strong>Note:</strong> When using authentication, you can drop off the <code>USERNAME</code> parameter and it will return the authenticated users'results.</p>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"api-method-description\">This method allows you the obtain all the check-in feed of the selected user. By default it will return at max 25 records.</p>\n\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<h4>Parameters</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<ul class=\"api-points\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>access_token</code> or <code>client_id</code> and <code>client_secret</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(string, required)</span> - Either pass the access_token for authorized calls OR the client_id and client_secret for unauthorized calls</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>USERNAME</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(string, optional)</span> - The username that you wish to call the request upon. Feed</h3>\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"page venueactivityfeed\" style=\"display: none;\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<ul class=\"api-points\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><strong>Authentication</strong>: Not Required</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><strong>HTTP Method</strong>: <code>GET</code></li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><strong>Endpoint</strong>: <code>/v4/venue/checkins/VENUE_ID</code></li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</ul>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"special-notice\"><strong>Note:</strong> This will return only users who have made their account public.</p>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"api-method-description\">is method allows you the obtain an activity feed for a single venue for Untappd. By default it will return at max 25 records.</p>\n\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<h4>Parameters</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<ul class=\"api-points\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>VENUE_ID</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(int, required)</span> - The Venue ID that you want to display checkins</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>access_token</code> or <code>client_id</code> and <code>client_secret</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(string, required)</span> - Either pass the access_token for authorized calls OR the client_id and client_secret for unauthorized calls</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>max_id</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(int, optional)</span> - The checkin ID that you want the results to start with</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>min_id</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(int, optional)</span> - Returns only checkins that are newer than this value</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>limit</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(int, optional)</span> - The number of results to return, max of 25, default is 25</li>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</ul>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<h4>Example Response</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div <code>GET</code></li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><strong>Endpoint</strong>: <code>/v4/user/beers/USERNAME</code></li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</ul>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"special-notice\"><strong>Note:</strong> When using authentication, you can drop off the <code>USERNAME</code> parameter and it will return the authenticated users'results.</p>\n\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"api-method-description\">This method will return a list of 25 of the user's distinct beers.</p>\n\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<h4>Parameters</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<ul class=\"api-points\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>USERNAME</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(string, optional)</span> - The username that you wish to call the request upon. Either pass the access_token for authorized calls OR the client_id and client_secret for unauthorized calls</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>offset</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(int, optional)</span> - sorts by global rating ascending order, <strong>highest_rated_you</strong> - the user's highest rated beer, <strong>lowest_rated_you</strong> - the user's lowest rated beer</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>start_date (string)</code> (To be used with End Date) To get all beers between this start_date and end_date (format: YYYY-MM-DD)</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>end_date (string)</code>(To be used with Start Date) To get all beers between the start_date and end_date (format: YYYY-MM-DD)</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</ul>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<h4>Example Response</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p></p><pre><code class=\"userBeerListJSON\">{\n  \"beers\": {\n    \"sort\": \"date\",\n    \"sort_english\": \"Date (Descending)\",\n    \"count\": 1,\n    \"items\": {\n      \"first_checkin_id\": 136912059,\n      \"first_created_at\": \"Fri, 12 Dec 2014 21:00:45 -0500\",\n      \"recent_checkin_id\": 136912059,\n      \"recent_created_at\": \"Fri, 12 Dec 2014 21:00:45 -0500\",\n      \"recent_created_at_timezone\": \"-5\",\n      \"rating_score\": 3.5,\n      \"first_had\": \"Fri, 12 Dec 2014 21:00:45 -0500\",\n      \"count\": 1,\n      \"beer\": {\n        \"bid\": 7807,\n        \"beer_name\": \"Christmas Ale\",\n        \"beer_label\": \"https://d1c8v1qci5en44.cloudfront.net/site/beer_logos/beer-_7807_1efa224bf295ec685c61d003dcd9.jpeg\",\n        \"beer_abv\": 6.1,\n        \"beer_ibu\": 0,\n        \"beer_slug\": \"abita-brewing-company-christmas-ale\",\n        \"beer_style\": \"Winter Ale\",\n        \"beer_description\": \"Abita Christmas Ale (November - <code>GET</code></li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><strong>Endpoint</strong>: <code>/v4/search/brewery</code></li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</ul>\n\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"api-method-description\">This will allow numeric offset that you what results to start</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>limit</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(int, optional)</span> - The number of results to return, max of 50, default is 25</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</ul>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<h4>Example Response</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"page checkin\" style=\"display: none;\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<ul class=\"api-points\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><strong>Authentication</strong>: Required</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><strong>HTTP Method</strong>: <code>POST</code></li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><strong>Endpoint</strong>: <code>/v4/checkin/add</code></li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</ul>\n\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"api-method-description\">This will allow you to check-in to a beer as the authenticated user</p>\n\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<h4>Parameters</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"activity box\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"api-info\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<ul class=\"api-points\">\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>access_token</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(string, required)</span> - The access token for the acting user</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>gmt_offset</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(string, required)</span> - The numeric value of hours the user is away from the GMT (Greenwich Mean Time), such as <code>-5</code>.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>timezone</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(string, required)</span> -  The timezone of the user, such as <code>EST</code> or <code>PST</code>./li&gt;\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</li><li><code>bid</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(int, required)</span> - The numeric Beer ID you want to check into.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>foursquare_id</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(string, optional)</span> - The MD5 hash ID of the Venue you want to attach the beer checkin. This HAS TO BE the MD5 non-numeric hash from the foursquare v2.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>geolat</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(int, optional)</span> -  The numeric Latitude of the user. This is required if you add a location.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>geolng</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(int, optional)</span> -  The numeric Longitude of the user. This is required if you add a location.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>shout</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(string, optional)</span> - The text you would like to include as a comment of the checkin. Max of 140 characters.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>rating</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(int, optional)</span> - The rating score you would like to add for the beer. This can only be 1 to 5 (half ratings are included). You can't rate a beer a 0.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>facebook</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(string, optional)</span> - If you want to push this check-in to the users' Facebook account, pass this value as \"on\", default is \"off\"</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>twitter</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(string, optional)</span> - If you want to push this check-in to the users' Twitter account, pass this value as \"on\", default is \"off\"</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><code>foursquare</code> <span class=\"req-block\">(string, optional)</span> - If you want to push this check-in to the users' Foursquare account, pass this value as \"on\", default is \"off\". You must include a location for this to enabled.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</ul>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"special-note\"><strong>Please Note</strong> It's possible that you could pass through a foursquare venue ID, and not get back a \"venue\" object in the response. This can be due to many reasons, but mainly due to a Foursquare connectivity issue. Your app or service should never depending on a one-to-one match on the foursquare ID send, and a venue object returned as part of the response. Always do a <code>null</code> check to make sure that the object's attributes exists before digging deeper into it.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<h4>Example
